• Developer Portal

Theatre Seating Layouts

V2 V3

Gets a list of a Theatre's auditoriums, and their seating layouts.
Note: An auditorium can have different seating layouts for different showtimes, with the id differentiating between them.

Endpoints

Verb Endpoint Description
GET /v2/theatres/{theatre-number}/seating-layouts Get Seating Layouts for an Auditorium.

Theatre Seating Layouts Properties

Name Description
theatreNumber The requested Theatre Number.
auditoriums The list of Auditoriums at the Theatre.

Theatre Seating Layouts Links

Relation Description Verbs Templated
self This auditorium's list of seating layouts GET No

Auditorium


Auditorium Properties

Name Description
auditorium The auditorium number.
layouts The list of layouts associated with the Auditorium.

Seating Layout


Seating Layout Properties

Name Description
theatreNumber The requested Theatre Number.
rows The total count of rows.
columns The total count of columns.
seats The list of seats in the layout.
id Differentiates between the various layouts an auditorium can have.
versionNumber The version of an auditorium layout. When a layout is changed, this will be incremented.

Seat


Seat Properties

Name Description
row The seat's row
column The seat's column
seatName The displayable seat name
type The type of seat
  • CanReserve
  • NotASeat (used to persist layout and designate isles)
  • Blocked
  • Wheelchair
  • Companion
  • GeneralAdmission
  • NA
  • LoveSeatLeft
  • LoveSeatRight
seatTier The tier a seat is targeted at.
  • [empty_string_when_non_seat]
  • Regular
  • Premiere


Examples

Get Auditorium Seating Layouts For at Theatre 38.
GET  /v2/theatres/38/seating-layouts
